country_event = {	# Pre Calculate AI Modifiers
    id = 20128
    title = "Calculate AI Modifiers!"
    #picture = "collectivisation"
	allow_multiple_instances = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {	# AI behaviour can be tuned in this event
		THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 1 } }
		THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 1 } }
		# More likely to support allies
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice alliance_with = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator alliance_with = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		# Less likely to support infamous states
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice badboy = 0.8 } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = -1 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator badboy = 0.8 } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = -1 } } }
		# More likely to support spherelings
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice in_sphere = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 3 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator in_sphere = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 3 } } }
		# More likely to support countries in culture groups
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice is_culture_group = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator is_culture_group = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		# More likely to support country with allies
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice num_of_allies = 3 } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator num_of_allies = 3 } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		# More likely to support country with prestige
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice prestige = 200 } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator prestige = 200 } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		# More likely to support friends
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice relation = { who = THIS value = 175 } } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator relation = { who = THIS value = 175 } } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 2 } } }
		# Less likely to support recent enemies
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice truce_with = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = -4 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator truce_with = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = -4 } } }
		# More likely to support vassals
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = scoped_for_dispute_choice vassal_of = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = scoped_for_dispute_choice_5_preference value = 3 } } }
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator vassal_of = THIS } THIS = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_initiator_choice_5_preference value = 3 } } }
	} 

	option = {
        name = ""
    }

}

country_event = { # Event to fire starting Cleanup event for CLN
    id = 20110
    title = "Bounce Event for GP where Arbitrator Rejects"
    #desc = ""
    #picture = "commonwealth"
	allow_multiple_instances = no
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = gp_current_dispute } set_country_flag = viewer }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = arbitration_initiator
			}
			set_variable = { which = country_loc_slot value = 1 }
		}
		country_event = 401
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gp_current_dispute
				NOT = { has_global_flag = Arbitration_5_setup_1_buffer_choice }
			}
			set_global_flag = Arbitration_5_setup_1_buffer_choice
		}
		any_country = { clr_country_flag = viewer }
	}
	
	option = {
        name = ""
    }
}
